# P00-15 Metric Catalogue

## Document Control

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Status | DRAFT-PENDING-PRODUCT-OPERATIONS-CLINICAL-SECURITY-PRIVACY-FINANCE-ACCESSIBILITY-AND-ENGINEERING-APPROVAL |
| Codex prompt ID | P00-15 |
| Complete Breakdown work package | P00-18 |
| Issue ID | P00-OPS-001 |
| Version | 0.1 draft |
| Owner | Operations owner |
| Review state | Draft pending external approval |
| Operational status | Proposed only; not implemented |
| Required reviewers | Product, operations, clinical, security, privacy, finance, accessibility, engineering, regulatory/legal, design, and content reviewers |
| Approval authority | External orchestration and named domain approvers |
| Last updated | 2026-06-25 |
| Effective date | NOT EFFECTIVE UNTIL APPROVED |
| Related decisions | REQ-OPS-001 through REQ-OPS-045 |
| Related open questions | OQ-00-675 through OQ-00-774 |
| Review and change control | Any target, threshold, dashboard audience, queue policy, stop decision, or analytics use change requires register update and external approval before production reliance. |

This document defines proposed metrics, service levels, queues, and pilot gates. It does not constitute an approved SLA, contractual service commitment, clinical response time, statutory or regulatory deadline, or staffing sufficiency statement. Numeric targets remain approval-controlled. Final instrumentation remains Phase 1 or later implementation work.


## Metric Design Principles

Outcome, process, safety, quality, reliability, financial-integrity, privacy, accessibility, experience, capacity, leading, lagging, countermetric, and guardrail metrics are defined as versioned measures of closed-loop operational outcomes. Metrics do not authorize clinical access, payment success, provider-detail access, credential approval, emergency closure, refund completion, patient switching, break-glass access, diagnosis, or treatment.

## Funnel and Closed-Loop Metrics

| Funnel | Start | Intermediate steps | Completion | Failure | Abandonment | Reopening | Owner | Countermetrics |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Registration to activated patient | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Booking to completed consultation | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Consultation to finalized disposition | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Prescription to completed fulfilment | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Diagnostic order to clinician-reviewed result | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Referral to documented outcome | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Emergency trigger to documented follow-up | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Payment initiation to reconciled transaction | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Refund request to completed original-source refund | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Provider onboarding to verified eligibility | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Complaint opening to approved closure | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |
| Critical result to documented resolution | Authoritative start event | Required workflow milestones | Safe documented closure | Exception queue or incident | Abandoned eligible flow | Reopened by corrected data, appeal, incident, or failed remediation | Operations/domain owner | Safety, privacy, clinical quality, finance integrity, accessibility, and disclosure guardrails |

## Prohibited or Misleading Standalone Metrics

Total page views, total app sessions, raw sign-ups, total prescriptions, total tests ordered, total medicine value, total provider-detail reveals, short consultation duration, low emergency escalation volume, low complaint volume, low incident reporting volume, high sponsor visibility, high employer member-level access, higher paid-order value, and higher platform fee without patient outcome context are contextual signals only. They are not proof that care worked.
